*Saugat Aryal,Mark T. Keane*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的可解释AI方法——信息性半事实解释（ISF），它不仅生成半事实解释（说明即使某些特征改变，预测结果仍保持不变），还补充了影响决策的隐藏特征信息，使解释更加丰富和有用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前半事实解释方法虽然能说明即使某些输入特征改变，预测结果仍保持不变，但无法解释为什么这些极端值变化不会改变结果。现有方法缺乏对影响决策的隐藏特征的说明，限制了半事实解释的信息价值。

Method: 提出信息性半事实解释（ISF）算法，该算法不仅生成传统的半事实解释（找到不改变结果的单个关键特征的最大值变化），还补充了影响自动化决策的隐藏特征信息，使解释更加详细和丰富。

Result: 在基准数据集上的实验结果表明，ISF方法生成的半事实解释既信息丰富，又在关键指标上具有高质量。用户研究显示，人们更喜欢这种详细解释，而不是现有方法生成的简单半事实解释。

Conclusion: ISF方法通过补充隐藏特征信息，显著提升了半事实解释的信息价值和实用性，为可解释AI提供了更丰富、更有用的解释工具，有助于用户更好地理解自动化决策背后的逻辑。

Abstract: Recently, in eXplainable AI (XAI), $\textit{even if}$ explanations -- so-called semi-factuals -- have emerged as a popular strategy that explains how a predicted outcome $\textit{can remain the same}$ even when certain input-features are altered. For example, in the commonly-used banking app scenario, a semi-factual explanation could inform customers about better options, other alternatives for their successful application, by saying "$\textit{Even if}$ you asked for double the loan amount, you would still be accepted". Most semi-factuals XAI algorithms focus on finding maximal value-changes to a single key-feature that do $\textit{not}$ alter the outcome (unlike counterfactual explanations that often find minimal value-changes to several features that alter the outcome). However, no current semi-factual method explains $\textit{why}$ these extreme value-changes do not alter outcomes; for example, a more informative semi-factual could tell the customer that it is their good credit score that allows them to borrow double their requested loan. In this work, we advance a new algorithm -- the $\textit{informative semi-factuals}$ (ISF) method -- that generates more elaborated explanations supplementing semi-factuals with information about additional $\textit{hidden features}$ that influence an automated decision. Experimental results on benchmark datasets show that this ISF method computes semi-factuals that are both informative and of high-quality on key metrics. Furthermore, a user study shows that people prefer these elaborated explanations over the simpler semi-factual explanations generated by current methods.

</details>


### [229] [Sensi: Learn One Thing at a Time -- Curriculum-Based Test-Time Learning for LLM Game Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17683)
*Mohsen Arjmandi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Sensi是一个用于ARC-AGI-3游戏挑战的LLM智能体架构，通过结构化测试时学习机制实现高效学习，相比现有系统提升50-94倍样本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体在未知环境中需要数千次交互才能形成有用假设，学习效率低下。需要开发能够在测试时高效学习的智能体架构。

Method: 提出Sensi架构，包含三个核心机制：1）感知与行动分离的双玩家架构；2）由外部状态机管理的课程学习系统；3）数据库作为控制平面实现程序化引导上下文窗口。还引入LLM作为评判者，动态生成评估标准。

Result: Sensi v1使用双玩家架构解决了2个游戏关卡。Sensi v2添加课程学习后解决了0个关卡，但仅用约32次行动尝试就完成了整个学习课程，相比需要1600-3000次尝试的同类系统，样本效率提升50-94倍。失败模式被诊断为感知层的自洽幻觉级联。

Conclusion: Sensi架构显著提升了测试时学习效率，将架构瓶颈从学习效率转移到感知基础问题，后者是更易处理的问题。展示了结构化学习机制在LLM智能体中的有效性。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents deployed in unknown environments must learn task structure at test time, but current approaches require thousands of interactions to form useful hypotheses. We present Sensi, an LLM agent architecture for the ARC-AGI-3 game-playing challenge that introduces structured test-time learning through three mechanisms: (1) a two-player architecture separating perception from action, (2) a curriculum-based learning system managed by an external state machine, and (3) a database-as-control-plane that makes the agents context window programmatically steerable. We further introduce an LLM-as-judge component with dynamically generated evaluation rubrics to determine when the agent has learned enough about one topic to advance to the next. We report results across two iterations: Sensi v1 solves 2 game levels using the two-player architecture alone, while Sensi v2 adds curriculum learning and solves 0 levels - but completes its entire learning curriculum in approximately 32 action attempts, achieving 50-94x greater sample efficiency than comparable systems that require 1600-3000 attempts. We precisely diagnose the failure mode as a self-consistent hallucination cascade originating in the perception layer, demonstrating that the architectural bottleneck has shifted from learning efficiency to perceptual grounding - a more tractable problem.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Central to our approach is a preference learning paradigm in which LLMs are economically aligned via post-training on extensive, heterogeneous transaction records across diverse product categories. This methodology enables the models to internalize and transfer latent consumer preference patterns, thereby mitigating the data sparsity issues prevalent in individual categories. To enhance simulation stability, we implement a mean-field mechanism designed to model the dynamic interactions between the product environment and customer populations, effectively stabilizing sampling processes within high-dimensional decision spaces. Furthermore, we propose a multi-agent discussion framework wherein specialized agents collaboratively process extensive product information. This architecture distributes cognitive load to alleviate single-agent attention bottlenecks and captures critical decision factors through structured dialogue. Experiments demonstrate that our framework achieves significant improvements in product selection accuracy, purchase quantity prediction, and simulation stability compared to existing economic and financial LLM simulation baselines. Our results substantiate the potential of large language models as a foundational pillar for high-fidelity, scalable decision simulation and latter analysis in the real economy based on foundational database.

We also highlight the role of vision-language models and simulation realism in enhancing scene understanding and generalization. ### [232] [Facts as First Class Objects: Knowledge Objects for Persistent LLM Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17781)
*Oliver Zahn,Simran Chana*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文比较了上下文记忆与知识对象两种知识存储方式，发现上下文记忆存在容量限制、压缩损失和目标漂移三大问题，而知识对象在成本、准确性和推理能力方面表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型越来越多地作为持久知识工作者使用，上下文记忆成为默认策略。然而，这种策略在实际部署中存在严重问题，需要探索更可靠的知识存储和检索方法。

Method: 研究对比了上下文记忆和知识对象两种方法。知识对象采用离散哈希寻址元组，具有O(1)检索复杂度。通过基准测试评估了两种方法在准确性、成本、多跳推理等方面的表现，并在四个前沿模型上进行了交叉验证。

Result: 上下文记忆在7,000个事实内能达到100%准确率，但存在三大失败模式：容量限制（8,000个事实时提示溢出）、压缩损失（摘要化破坏60%事实）、目标漂移（级联压缩侵蚀54%项目约束）。知识对象在所有条件下保持100%准确率，成本降低252倍，多跳推理达到78.9%（上下文记忆仅31.6%）。

Conclusion: 上下文记忆存在架构性缺陷，不适合大规模知识存储。知识对象提供了更可靠、高效的知识管理方案，并引入了密度自适应检索作为切换机制。研究还发现嵌入检索在对抗性事实上表现不佳，神经记忆能存储但无法按需检索。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly serve as persistent knowledge workers, with in-context memory - facts stored in the prompt - as the default strategy. We benchmark in-context memory against Knowledge Objects (KOs), discrete hash-addressed tuples with O(1) retrieval. Within the context window, Claude Sonnet 4.5 achieves 100% exact-match accuracy from 10 to 7,000 facts (97.5% of its 200K window). However, production deployment reveals three failure modes: capacity limits (prompts overflow at 8,000 facts), compaction loss (summarization destroys 60% of facts), and goal drift (cascading compaction erodes 54% of project constraints while the model continues with full confidence). KOs achieve 100% accuracy across all conditions at 252x lower cost. On multi-hop reasoning, KOs reach 78.9% versus 31.6% for in-context. Cross-model replication across four frontier models confirms compaction loss is architectural, not model-specific. We additionally show that embedding retrieval fails on adversarial facts (20% precision at 1) and that neural memory (Titans) stores facts but fails to retrieve them on demand. We introduce density-adaptive retrieval as a switching mechanism and release the benchmark suite.

</details>


### [233] [AgentFactory: A Self-Evolving Framework Through Executable Subagent Accumulation and Reuse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18000)
*Zhang Zhang,Shuqi Lu,Hongjin Qian,Di He,Zheng Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentFactory提出了一种新的LLM智能体自进化范式，将成功任务解决方案保存为可执行的子智能体代码而非文本经验，实现持续能力积累。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体自进化方法主要将成功经验记录为文本提示或反思，这在复杂场景中无法可靠保证任务的高效重新执行，需要更可靠的进化机制。

Method: 提出AgentFactory框架，将成功任务解决方案保存为可执行的子智能体Python代码，这些子智能体基于执行反馈持续优化，具有标准化文档和跨系统可移植性。

Result: AgentFactory实现了持续能力积累，其可执行子智能体库随时间增长和改进，逐步减少类似任务所需的工作量，无需人工干预。

Conclusion: AgentFactory通过将成功经验编码为可执行代码而非文本，为LLM智能体自进化提供了更可靠、可移植的解决方案，支持持续能力积累和效率提升。

Abstract: Building LLM-based agents has become increasingly important. Recent works on LLM-based agent self-evolution primarily record successful experiences as textual prompts or reflections, which cannot reliably guarantee efficient task re-execution in complex scenarios. We propose AgentFactory, a new self-evolution paradigm that preserves successful task solutions as executable subagent code rather than textual experience. Crucially, these subagents are continuously refined based on execution feedback, becoming increasingly robust and efficient as more tasks are encountered. Saved subagents are pure Python code with standardized documentation, enabling portability across any Python-capable system. We demonstrate that AgentFactory enables continuous capability accumulation: its library of executable subagents grows and improves over time, progressively reducing the effort required for similar tasks without manual intervention. Our implementation is open-sourced at https://github.com/zzatpku/AgentFactory, and our demonstration video is available at https://youtu.be/iKSsuAXJHW0.

</details>

### [234] [OPERA: Online Data Pruning for Efficient Retrieval Model Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17205)
*Haoyang Fang,Shuai Zhang,Yifei Ma,Hengyi Wang,Cuixiong Hu,Katrin Kirchhoff,Bernie Wang,George Karypis*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: OPERA是一个数据剪枝框架，通过利用训练数据的异质性来提高检索模型微调的效率和效果，包括静态剪枝和动态剪枝两种策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 领域特定的微调对密集检索器至关重要，但并非所有训练数据对都对学习过程有同等贡献。现有方法在处理训练数据异质性方面存在不足，需要更有效的数据选择策略来平衡质量和覆盖率。

Method: 提出OPERA数据剪枝框架：1）静态剪枝（SP）：仅保留高相似度的查询-文档对；2）动态剪枝（DP）：两阶段策略，在训练过程中自适应调整查询和文档级别的采样概率，优先高质量样本同时保持对完整训练集的访问。

Result: 在6个领域的8个数据集上评估：SP相比标准微调在排名指标上提升（NDCG@10 +0.5%），DP在排名（NDCG@10 +1.9%）和检索（Recall@20 +0.7%）上都表现最强，平均排名1.38。DP仅需标准微调不到50%的训练时间就能达到可比性能，且结果在Qwen3-Embedding等LLM基密集检索器上也得到验证。

Conclusion: OPERA框架通过数据剪枝有效解决了训练数据异质性问题，动态剪枝策略在保持查询多样性的同时优先高质量样本，实现了效果和效率的双重提升，且具有架构无关的通用性。

Abstract: Domain-specific finetuning is essential for dense retrievers, yet not all training pairs contribute equally to the learning process. We introduce OPERA, a data pruning framework that exploits this heterogeneity to improve both the effectiveness and efficiency of retrieval model adaptation. We first investigate static pruning (SP), which retains only high-similarity query-document pairs, revealing an intrinsic quality-coverage tradeoff: ranking (NDCG) improves while retrieval (Recall) can degrade due to reduced query diversity. To resolve this tradeoff, we propose a two-stage dynamic pruning (DP) strategy that adaptively modulates sampling probabilities at both query and document levels throughout training, prioritizing high-quality examples while maintaining access to the full training set. Evaluations across eight datasets spanning six domains demonstrate the effectiveness of both approaches: SP improves ranking over standard finetuning (NDCG@10 +0.5\%), while DP achieves the strongest performance on both ranking (NDCG@10 +1.9\%) and retrieval (Recall@20 +0.7\%), with an average rank of 1.38 across all methods. These findings scale to Qwen3-Embedding, an LLM-based dense retriever, confirming architecture-agnostic benefits. Notably, DP reaches comparable performance in less than 50\% of the training time required by standard finetuning.

</details>

*Chunxu Zhang,Zhiheng Xue,Guodong Long,Weipeng Zhang,Bo Yang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: FCUCR是一个联邦持续推荐框架，通过时间感知自蒸馏策略解决时间遗忘问题，并通过用户间原型转移机制增强协作个性化，在保护隐私的同时实现长期个性化推荐。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出FCUCR联邦持续推荐框架：1) 时间感知自蒸馏策略，在本地模型更新时隐式保留历史偏好；2) 用户间原型转移机制，利用相似用户知识丰富客户端表示，同时保留个体决策逻辑。

Result: 在四个公共基准测试上的广泛实验表明，该方法具有优越的有效性，同时具备强大的兼容性和实际适用性。

Conclusion: FCUCR框架成功解决了联邦推荐中的时间遗忘和协作个性化问题，在保护隐私的同时实现了长期个性化推荐，代码已开源。

Abstract: User-centric recommendation has become essential for delivering personalized services, as it enables systems to adapt to users' evolving behaviors while respecting their long-term preferences and privacy constraints. Although federated learning offers a promising alternative to centralized training, existing approaches largely overlook user behavior dynamics, leading to temporal forgetting and weakened collaborative personalization. In this work, we propose FCUCR, a federated continual recommendation framework designed to support long-term personalization in a privacy-preserving manner. To address temporal forgetting, we introduce a time-aware self-distillation strategy that implicitly retains historical preferences during local model updates. To tackle collaborative personalization under heterogeneous user data, we design an inter-user prototype transfer mechanism that enriches each client's representation using knowledge from similar users while preserving individual decision logic. Extensive experiments on four public benchmarks demonstrate the superior effectiveness of our approach, along with strong compatibility and practical applicability. Code is available.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统对比学习范式在推理密集型检索中存在局限：它只能将层次相关性概念编码为向量空间中的固定几何结构，无法根据每个查询的具体推理需求动态调整相关性判断。当查询与文档存在词汇不匹配或需要隐式推理建立相关性时，性能会明显下降。

Method: 提出T1生成式检索模型，将相关性建模从静态对齐转向动态推理。查询侧：为每个查询动态生成中间推理轨迹以桥接隐式推理关系，使用<embtoken>作为推理输出的语义聚合点。文档侧：采用"指令+文本+<embtoken>"编码格式支持高吞吐量索引。通过三阶段训练课程，在第三阶段引入GRPO，使模型能通过试错强化学习学习不同查询的最优推导策略。

Result: 在BRIGHT基准测试中，T1-4B模型在原始查询设置下表现出色，总体上优于使用对比学习训练的更大模型，并实现了与多阶段检索管道相当的性能。

Conclusion: 用动态推理生成取代静态表示对齐能有效提升推理密集型检索性能，T1模型通过生成中间推理轨迹和强化学习训练策略，成功解决了传统检索方法在隐式推理关系识别上的局限性。

Abstract: The central challenge of reasoning-intensive retrieval lies in identifying implicitreasoning relationships between queries and documents, rather than superficial se-mantic or lexical similarity. The contrastive learning paradigm is fundamentallya static representation consolidation technique: during training, it encodes hier-archical relevance concepts into fixed geometric structures in the vector space,and at inference time it cannot dynamically adjust relevance judgments accord-ing to the specific reasoning demands of each query. Consequently, performancedegrades noticeably when vocabulary mismatch exists between queries and doc-uments or when implicit reasoning is required to establish relevance. This pa-per proposes Thought 1 (T1), a generative retrieval model that shifts relevancemodeling from static alignment to dynamic reasoning. On the query side, T1 dy-namically generates intermediate reasoning trajectories for each query to bridgeimplicit reasoning relationships and uses <embtoken> as a semantic aggregationpoint for the reasoning output. On the document side, it employs an instruction+ text + <embtoken> encoding format to support high-throughput indexing. Tointernalize dynamic reasoning capabilities into vector representations, we adopt athree-stage training curriculum and introduce GRPO in the third stage, enablingthe model to learn optimal derivation strategies for different queries through trial-and-error reinforcement learning. On the BRIGHT benchmark, T1-4B exhibitsstrong performance under the original query setting, outperforming larger modelstrained with contrastive learning overall, and achieving performance comparableto multi-stage retrieval pipelines. The results demonstrate that replacing static rep-resentation alignment with dynamic reasoning generation can effectively improvereasoning-intensive retrieval performance.

</details>


### [238] [VLM2Rec: Resolving Modality Collapse in Vision-Language Model Embedders for Multimodal Sequential Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17450)
*Junyoung Kim,Woojoo Kim,Jaehyung Lim,Dongha Kim,Hwanjo Yu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: VLM2Rec框架使用视觉语言模型作为协同过滤感知的多模态编码器，通过弱模态惩罚对比学习和跨模态关系拓扑正则化解决模态崩溃问题，提升多模态序列推荐性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态序列推荐通常依赖小型冻结预训练编码器，限制了语义容量，无法将协同过滤信号充分整合到物品表示中。虽然大型语言模型作为高容量嵌入器取得了成功，但视觉语言模型在标准对比监督微调下会出现模态崩溃问题。

Method: 提出VLM2Rec框架：1) 弱模态惩罚对比学习，纠正优化过程中的梯度不平衡；2) 跨模态关系拓扑正则化，保持模态间的几何一致性。确保多模态的平衡利用。

Result: 大量实验表明，VLM2Rec在多样场景下，在准确性和鲁棒性方面持续优于最先进的基线方法。

Conclusion: VLM2Rec成功解决了视觉语言模型在多模态序列推荐中的模态崩溃问题，通过平衡多模态利用显著提升了推荐性能，为使用高容量多模态编码器进行协同过滤感知的序列推荐提供了有效框架。

Abstract: Sequential Recommendation (SR) in multimodal settings typically relies on small frozen pretrained encoders, which limits semantic capacity and prevents Collaborative Filtering (CF) signals from being fully integrated into item representations. Inspired by the recent success of Large Language Models (LLMs) as high-capacity embedders, we investigate the use of Vision-Language Models (VLMs) as CF-aware multimodal encoders for SR. However, we find that standard contrastive supervised fine-tuning (SFT), which adapts VLMs for embedding generation and injects CF signals, can amplify its inherent modality collapse. In this state, optimization is dominated by a single modality while the other degrades, ultimately undermining recommendation accuracy. To address this, we propose VLM2Rec, a VLM embedder-based framework for multimodal sequential recommendation designed to ensure balanced modality utilization. Specifically, we introduce Weak-modality Penalized Contrastive Learning to rectify gradient imbalance during optimization and Cross-Modal Relational Topology Regularization to preserve geometric consistency between modalities. Extensive experiments demonstrate that VLM2Rec consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in both accuracy and robustness across diverse scenarios.

</details>


### [239] [A Unified Language Model for Large Scale Search, Recommendation, and Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17533)
*Marco De Nadai,Edoardo D'Amico,Max Lefarov,Alexandre Tamborrino,Divita Vohra,Mark VanMiddlesworth,Shawn Lin,Jacqueline Wood,Jan Stypka,Eliza Klyce,Keshi Dai,Timothy Christopher Heath,Martin D. Gould,Yves Raimond,Sandeep Ghael,Tony Jebara,Andreas Damianou,Vladan Radosavljevic,Paul N. Bennett,Mounia Lalmas,Praveen Chandar*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: NEO是一个将预训练LLM转换为无需工具、基于目录的生成器框架，通过SID表示商品并训练单一模型在共享序列中交错自然语言和类型化商品标识符，实现推荐、搜索和用户理解等多任务统一处理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM在推荐、检索和推理应用中面临挑战：需要生成对真实商品的无歧义引用、处理多种实体类型、满足严格的延迟和可靠性要求。工具增强的推荐系统虽然部分解决了问题，但引入了编排复杂性并限制了端到端优化。

Method: 提出NEO框架，将预训练解码器LLM转换为工具无关的目录基础生成器。使用SID表示商品，训练单一模型在共享序列中交错自然语言和类型化商品标识符。通过文本提示控制任务、目标实体类型和输出格式，约束解码保证生成有效的目录商品而不限制自由文本。

Result: 在包含1000万+商品的真实世界目录上进行评估，NEO在推荐、搜索和用户理解等发现任务中持续优于强任务特定基线，并展现出跨任务迁移能力。

Conclusion: NEO展示了将大规模发现能力整合到单一语言可操控生成模型中的实用路径，通过将SID作为不同模态并通过分阶段对齐和指令调优集成离散实体表示，实现了语言可操控性。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly applied to recommendation, retrieval, and reasoning, yet deploying a single end-to-end model that can jointly support these behaviors over large, heterogeneous catalogs remains challenging. Such systems must generate unambiguous references to real items, handle multiple entity types, and operate under strict latency and reliability constraints requirements that are difficult to satisfy with text-only generation. While tool-augmented recommender systems address parts of this problem, they introduce orchestration complexity and limit end-to-end optimization. We view this setting as an instance of a broader research problem: how to adapt LLMs to reason jointly over multiple-domain entities, users, and language in a fully self-contained manner. To this end, we introduce NEO, a framework that adapts a pre-trained decoder-only LLM into a tool-free, catalog-grounded generator. NEO represents items as SIDs and trains a single model to interleave natural language and typed item identifiers within a shared sequence. Text prompts control the task, target entity type, and output format (IDs, text, or mixed), while constrained decoding guarantees catalog-valid item generation without restricting free-form text. We refer to this instruction-conditioned controllability as language-steerability. We treat SIDs as a distinct modality and study design choices for integrating discrete entity representations into LLMs via staged alignment and instruction tuning. We evaluate NEO at scale on a real-world catalog of over 10M items across multiple media types and discovery tasks, including recommendation, search, and user understanding. In offline experiments, NEO consistently outperforms strong task-specific baselines and exhibits cross-task transfer, demonstrating a practical path toward consolidating large-scale discovery capabilities into a single language-steerable generative model.

</details>


### [240] [Deploying Semantic ID-based Generative Retrieval for Large-Scale Podcast Discovery at Spotify](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17540)
*Edoardo D'Amico,Marco De Nadai,Praveen Chandar,Divita Vohra,Shawn Lin,Max Lefarov,Paul Gigioli,Gustavo Penha,Ilya Kopysitsky,Ivo Joel Senese,Darren Mei,Francesco Fabbri,Oguz Semerci,Yu Zhao,Vincent Tang,Brian St. Thomas,Alexandra Ranieri,Matthew N. Method: GLIDE将推荐制定为基于语义ID的指令跟随任务，使用离散化播客目录进行接地生成。模型条件化最近收听历史和轻量级用户上下文，同时注入长期用户嵌入作为软提示，在严格推理约束下捕捉稳定偏好

Result: 通过离线检索指标、人工判断和基于LLM的评估，以及大规模在线A/B测试验证，GLIDE在涉及数百万用户的实验中，将Spotify首页的非习惯性播客流媒体播放量提升高达5.4%，新节目发现提升高达14.3%，同时满足生产成本和延迟约束

Abstract: Podcast listening is often grounded in a set of favorite shows, while listener intent can evolve over time. This combination of stable preferences and changing intent motivates recommendation approaches that support both familiarity and exploration. Traditional recommender systems typically emphasize long-term interaction patterns, and are less explicitly designed to incorporate rich contextual signals or flexible, intent-aware discovery objectives. In this setting, models that can jointly reason over semantics, context, and user state offer a promising direction. Large Language Models (LLMs) provide strong semantic reasoning and contextual conditioning for discovery-oriented recommendation, but deploying them in production introduces challenges in catalog grounding, user-level personalization, and latency-critical serving.
  We address these challenges with GLIDE, a production-scale generative recommender for podcast discovery at Spotify. GLIDE formulates recommendation as an instruction-following task over a discretized catalog using Semantic IDs, enabling grounded generation over a large inventory. The model conditions on recent listening history and lightweight user context, while injecting long-term user embeddings as soft prompts to capture stable preferences under strict inference constraints. We evaluate GLIDE using offline retrieval metrics, human judgments, and LLM-based evaluation, and validate its impact through large-scale online A/B testing. Across experiments involving millions of users, GLIDE increases non-habitual podcast streaming on Spotify home surface by up to 5.4% and new-show discovery by up to 14.3%, while meeting production cost and latency constraints.

### [241] [From Isolated Scoring to Collaborative Ranking: A Comparison-Native Framework for LLM-Based Paper Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17588)
*Pujun Zheng,Jiacheng Yao,Jinquan Zheng,Chenyang Gu,Guoxiu He,Jiawei Liu,Yong Huang,Tianrui Guo,Wei Lu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出CNPE框架，将论文评估从独立评分转向协同排名，通过图相似性算法构建论文对，结合监督微调和强化学习训练模型，在推理时通过成对比较生成全局质量排名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型用于论文评估时采用独立绝对评分，但评分标准因会议、时间、标准而异，模型容易过拟合特定上下文规则而非发展稳健的学术判断能力。

Method: 提出CNPE框架：1) 基于图的相似性排名算法采样信息量更大、区分度更高的论文对；2) 通过监督微调和基于比较奖励的强化学习增强相对质量判断；3) 推理时对采样的论文对进行成对比较，聚合偏好信号生成全局相对质量排名。

Result: 实验结果显示，该框架相比强基线DeepReview-14B平均相对提升21.8%，并在五个未见数据集上展现出稳健的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 将论文评估从孤立评分转向协同排名的方法能有效提升模型的评估质量和泛化能力，CNPE框架为解决绝对评分标准不一致问题提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are currently applied to scientific paper evaluation by assigning an absolute score to each paper independently. However, since score scales vary across conferences, time periods, and evaluation criteria, models trained on absolute scores are prone to fitting narrow, context-specific rules rather than developing robust scholarly judgment. To overcome this limitation, we propose shifting paper evaluation from isolated scoring to collaborative ranking. In particular, we design \textbf{C}omparison-\textbf{N}ative framework for \textbf{P}aper \textbf{E}valuation (\textbf{CNPE}), integrating comparison into both data construction and model learning. We first propose a graph-based similarity ranking algorithm to facilitate the sampling of more informative and discriminative paper pairs from a collection. We then enhance relative quality judgment through supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning with comparison-based rewards. At inference, the model performs pairwise comparisons over sampled paper pairs and aggregates these preference signals into a global relative quality ranking. Experimental results demonstrate that our framework achieves an average relative improvement of \textbf{21.8\%} over the strong baseline DeepReview-14B, while exhibiting robust generalization to five previously unseen datasets. \href{https://github.com/ECNU-Text-Computing/ComparisonReview}{Code}.

</details>


### [242] [A Contextual Help Browser Extension to Assist Digital Illiterate Internet Users](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17592)
*Christos Koutsiaris*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 开发了一个浏览器扩展，通过悬停工具提示为网页上的技术缩写提供上下文帮助，结合了技术词典和AI模型，显著提升了用户理解并节省了搜索时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决数字素养较低用户在浏览网页时遇到技术缩写和首字母缩略词的理解障碍，减少他们需要中断阅读进行手动搜索的时间成本。

Method: 开发浏览器扩展，采用双层级AI管道：先用Google Cloud NLP API分类网页是否为技术相关，再激活工具提示逻辑。工具提示结合了技术词典和OpenAI的LLM，通过轻量级覆盖层提供定义。

Result: 25名参与者的混合方法研究显示：92%报告对技术术语理解改善，96%确认相比手动网页搜索节省时间，所有参与者认为工具提示不具干扰性。词典定义平均2135ms，AI生成定义16429ms，手动搜索平均17200ms。

Conclusion: 该工具提供了一种实用的实时方法来解决数字素养差距，显著改善了技术术语的理解效率，并展示了扩展到医学、法律、金融等其他领域的潜力。

Abstract: This paper describes the design, implementation, and evaluation of a browser extension that provides contextual help to users who hover over technological acronyms and abbreviations on web pages. The extension combines a curated technical dictionary with OpenAI's large language model (LLM) to deliver on-demand definitions through lightweight tooltip overlays. A dual-layer artificial intelligence (AI) pipeline, comprising Google Cloud's Natural Language Processing (NLP) taxonomy API and OpenAI's ChatGPT, classifies each visited page as technology-related before activating the tooltip logic, thereby reducing false-positive detections. A mixed-methods study with 25 participants evaluated the tool's effect on reading comprehension and information-retrieval time among users with low to intermediate digital literacy. Results show that 92% of participants reported improved understanding of technical terms, 96% confirmed time savings over manual web searches, and all participants found the tooltips non-disruptive. Dictionary-based definitions were appended in an average of 2135 ms, compared to 16429 ms for AI-generated definitions and a mean manual search time of 17200 ms per acronym. The work demonstrates a practical, real-time approach to bridging the digital literacy gap and points toward extending contextual help to other domains such as medicine, law, and finance.

</details>

### [243] [An approximation notion between P and FPTAS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17489)
*Samuel Bismuth,Erel Segal-Halevi*

Main category: cs.CC

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于NP难优化问题的新近似概念，证明其严格强于FPTAS但严格弱于多项式时间算法


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对NP难优化问题，现有近似算法概念存在局限性，需要更精细的近似概念来区分不同问题的可近似性

Method: 提出新的近似概念，基于二进制函数表示NP难优化问题，通过理论分析证明该概念与现有近似概念的关系

Result: 证明新近似概念严格强于FPTAS（完全多项式时间近似方案），但严格弱于多项式时间精确算法

Conclusion: 该新近似概念为NP难优化问题提供了更精细的近似性分类，填补了FPTAS和多项式时间精确算法之间的空白

Abstract: We present an approximation notion for NP-hard optimization problems represented by binary functions. We prove that (assuming P != NP) the new notion is strictly stronger than FPTAS, but strictly weaker than having a polynomial-time algorithm.

</details>
